ncu	Kufwiiri‑o kamɛɛ, Nowaa mò̱ agyi
ncu	nyaŋsɛ, Sɛm na Ham na Yafɛt, a
ncu	kye̱na ko̱we̱ agyi. Yafɛt e̱ gye̱
ncu	mò̱ bregyi, ne̱ Sɛm gya mò̱
ncu	se̱, ne̱ Ham e̱ gye̱
ncu	kalo̱we̱.Yafɛt na mò̱ ananagyi
ncu	Ane̱ŋ ne̱ Nowaa mò̱ gyi‑ana na
ncu	mò̱ ananagyi anyare̱ ke̱gyase̱
ncu	ke̱gyase̱ du‑o ne̱e̱. Ane̱ŋ
ncu	ne̱ baa kye̱na nsuro si nsuro si na
ncu	mbuno si mbuno si‑o ne̱e̱.
ncu	Kufwiiri‑o kamɛɛ, bamo̱ ya
ncu	brawe̱‑rɔ bo̱rɔ kaye̱‑rɔ
ncu	to̱ŋ ke̱maa ke̱maa‑ɔ.
ncu	Sarayi fe̱raa mo̱ŋ ko̱we̱, ɔ
ncu	gye̱ ɔle̱ŋmaŋpo̱ ne̱e̱.
ncu	Kake ŋko̱ ne̱ Abram na Lɔt a mbo̱
ncu	ade̱e̱re̱se̱po̱‑ɔ a nya
ncu	se̱ŋsa. Saŋ amo̱ Kanaŋ awuye na
ncu	Pɛrisi awuye‑o mɔ te
ncu	swe̱e̱re̱‑ɔ dɛɛ se̱.
ncu	ne̱ aa yure Abram tɔwe̱

ncu	ɛɛ-Bware̱,mò̱ ne̱ aa twe̱e̱
ncu	so̱so̱ na kaase̱‑ɔ, yure Abram.
ncu	Amo̱se̱‑ɔ Abram nsu kudu Kanaŋ
ncu	swe̱e̱re̱ se̱, ne̱ mò̱ ka

ncu	mò̱ kuri na ɔ bo̱ waa mò̱ ka.
ncu	Abraham da swe̱e̱re̱ na mò̱
ncu	akatɔ‑rɔ buŋ swe̱e̱re̱, ne̱ aa
ncu	mɔse̱, ne̱ aa fa mò̱
ncu	mfɛɛre̱‑rɔ fɛɛ, “Ɔnyare̱
ncu	ne̱ aa gyi nsu ke̱lafa‑ɔ be̱e̱
ncu	ɔ taare̱ a ɔ ko̱we̱ gyi nyaŋsɛ
ncu	aaa? Sara ne̱ aa gyi nsu
ncu	adukpɔnɔɔ‑ɔ be̱e̱ ɔ taare̱ a
ncu	ɔ nya kame ko̱we̱ aaa?”
ncu	Sɔdɔm na Gomora awuye
ncu	bo̱ro̱kɔɔne̱ a waa ko̱kyɔ mo̱
ncu	ase̱, amo̱se̱‑ɔ mo̱ duŋ a fwii
ncu	Anyare̱ amo̱ a de̱ŋ lee bamo̱
ncu	le̱e̱ maŋ‑ɔ‑rɔ lo̱we̱‑ɔ,
ncu	ne̱ bamo̱ ɔko̱ yɛ, “Mo̱nꞌ
ncu	se̱re̱ keŋkeŋ nare̱! Mo̱ne̱ ma
ncu	nyɔŋ ke̱e̱, na mo̱ne̱ ma ye̱re̱
ncu	ifuri mɔ se̱ to̱ŋ ko̱! Mo̱nꞌ
ncu	se̱re̱ nare̱ abe̱e̱‑ɔ‑rɔ na
ncu	mo̱ne̱ ma nya tii ase̱sɛ
ncu	Ne̱ aa te̱e̱ e̱se̱‑ɔ fɛɛ
ncu	swe̱e̱re̱,ne̱ aa te̱e̱ nkyu ne̱
ncu	ɔpo̱o̱.Ne̱ Wuribware̱ a ŋu fɛɛ

ncu	ne̱ aa bise mò̱ fɛɛ, “Nte̱tɔ

ncu	fo̱ a sa ne̱ mo̱ aa mo̱ ase̱sɛ a
ncu	gyi ke̱pɔ ke̱baŋse̱ mɔ? Fo̱
ncu	mo̱ŋ waa nɛɛnɛɛ. Fo̱ a waa mo̱
ncu	atɔ ne̱ a mo̱ŋ bware fɛɛ fo̱

ncu	ke̱tɔ ke̱maa ne̱ fo̱ e̱
ncu	Mo̱ e̱ bo̱rɔ fo̱ ananagyi‑o si a
ncu	ŋ yure ase̱sɛ pɛɛɛ ne̱ bo̱ bo̱
ncu	kaye̱‑rɔ‑ɔ, bo̱ le̱e̱ fɛɛ
ncu	fo̱ a gya mo̱ kanɔ se̱.”
ncu	Mo̱ e̱ kpa fɛɛ fo̱ waa Wuribware̱
ncu	ne̱ aa twe̱e̱ so̱so̱ na
ncu	swe̱e̱re̱‑ɔ e̱taŋ fɛɛ fo̱
ncu	maa kpa kye̱e̱ a fo̱ le̱e̱ Kanaŋ
ncu	mfe̱e̱ a ase̱sɛ‑ɔ ase̱ a fo̱

ncu	bwe̱e̱tɔ, ne̱ aa kii atɔ wuye. Aa
ncu	sa mò̱ e̱sanne̱ na e̱naate̱ na
ncu	atanne̱ fufuri na apipee na
ncu	ayaafɔre̱ na mbregyii na e̱nyɔma na

ncu	mò̱ ka, ne̱ Isak a kpa mò̱
ncu	bwe̱e̱tɔ, ne̱ aa gyi mò̱ akatɔ
ncu	mò̱ nyi Sara lowi kamɛɛ.
ncu	Ne̱ Yakubu a be̱ŋŋaa mò̱ fɛɛ,

ncu	Ne̱ Isak a bise bamo̱ ɛ, “Mo̱ne̱

ncu	le̱e̱ mo̱ne̱ ase̱, ne̱ ntɔ ne̱
ncu	mo̱ne̱ e̱ kpa mo̱ ase̱ mfe̱e̱?”

ncu	Ɔbre̱sɛ‑ɔ e̱ gye̱ Leya, ne̱

ncu	Bo̱ŋ‑ɔ kuŋu gye̱ŋkpɛɛsɛ‑ɔ

ncu	bo̱ sɔɔ ndɔɔ a kadike‑o.”

ncu	Mo̱‑kigyisesare̱e̱‑se̱-gyi.

ncu	ayaa asa na ke̱be̱gya na

ncu	mò̱ ŋkpaŋŋe̱‑rɔ mɔ waa ayaa

ncu	mò̱ ananagyi nsu pɛɛɛ.”
